167→\treturn true\n   168→}\n   169→\n   170→func (svmc *SVMController) sync(ctx context.Context, key string) error {\n   171→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   172→\tstartTime := time.Now()\n 279→\t\ttypeMeta.UID = accessor.GetUID()\n   280→\t\t// set RV so that when a resources gets updated or deleted+recreated, we get an \"object has been modified\"\n   281→\t\t// conflict error.  we do not actually need to do anything special for the updated case because if RV\n   282→\t\t// was not set, it would just result in no-op request.  but for the deleted+recreated case, if RV is\n   283→\t\t// not set but UID is set, we would get an immutable field validation error.  hence we must set both.\n   284→\t\ttypeMeta.ResourceVersion = accessor.GetResourceVersion()\n   285→\t\tdata, err 291→\t\t\tNamespace(accessor.GetNamespace()).\n   292→\t\t\tPatch(ctx,\n   293→\t\t\t\taccessor.GetName(),\n   294→\t\t\t\ttypes.ApplyPatchType,\n   295→\t\t\t\tdata,\n   296→\t\t\t\tmetav1.PatchOptions{\n   297→\t\t\t\t\tFieldManager: svmc.controllerName,\n   298→\t\t\t\t},\n   299→\t\t\t)\n   300→\n   301→\t\t// in case of conflict, we can stop processing migration for that resource because it has either been\n   302→\t\t// - updated, meaning that migration has already been performed\n   303→\t\t// - deleted, meaning that migration is not needed\n   304→\t\t// - deleted and recreated, meaning that migration has already been performed\n   305→\t\tif apierrors.IsConflict(errPatch) {\n   306→\t\t\tlogger.V(6).Info(\"Resource ignored due to conflict\", 311→\t\t\tlogger.V(4).Error(errPatch, \"Failed to migrate the resource\", \"namespace\", accessor.GetNamespace(), \"name\", accessor.GetName(), \"gvr\", gvr.String(), \"reason\", 316→\t\t\t\t\tctx,\n   317→\t\t\t\t\tsetStatusConditions(toBeProcessedSVM, svmv1alpha1.MigrationFailed, migrationFailedStatusReason, \"migration encountered unhandled error\"),\n   318→\t\t\t\t\tmetav1.UpdateOptions{},\n   319→\t\t\t\t)\n   320→\n   321→\t\t\treturn errStatus\n   322→\t\t\t// Todo: add retry for scenarios where API server returns rate limiting error\n   323→\t\t}\n   324→\t\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"Successfully migrated the resource\", \"namespace\", accessor.GetNamespace(), \"name\", accessor.GetName(), \"gvr\", gvr.String())\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\t_, err = svmc.kubeClient.StoragemigrationV1alpha1().\n   328→\t\tStorageVersionMigrations().\n   329→\t\tUpdateStatus(\n   330→\t\t\tctx,\n   331→\t\t\tsetStatusConditions(toBeProcessedSVM, 338→\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"Finished syncing svm resource\", \"key\", key, \"gvr\", gvr.String(), \"elapsed\", time.Since(startTime))\n   339→\treturn nil\n   340→}\n   341→\n   342→type typeMetaUIDRV accessor.GetUID()\n\t\t// set RV so that when a resources gets updated or deleted+recreated, we get an \"object has been modified\"\n\t\t// conflict error.  we do not actually need to do anything \"text\": \"The kubernetes/kubernetes codebase (v1.32.0) does not use the external sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime library. Instead, it implements its own controller manager framework via the staged k8s.io/controller-manager package and the kube-controller-manager app. Here is how a controller registers itself with the Manager's reconcile loop:\\n\\n1. **Reconciler Interface** (`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`): The `controller.Interface` is the base interface every controller must satisfy, requiring only `Name() string`. Additional optional interfaces include `Debuggable` (for debug HTTP handlers) and `HealthCheckable` (for health check endpoints). Individual controllers implement a `syncXxx` or internal reconcile method as their core reconcile logic.\\n\\n2. **SetupWithManager equivalent — InitFunc & ControllerDescriptor** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): Each controller defines a `ControllerDescriptor` struct that pairs a controller name with an `InitFunc`. The `InitFunc` type (`func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error)`) is the analogue of `SetupWithManager` — it instantiates the controller, wires it to informers/clients from `ControllerContext`, starts its goroutine, and returns the controller instance. For example, `startEndpointsController` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/core.go` creates an `EndpointController` and calls `go ... .Run(ctx, workers)`.\\n\\n3. **Registration — NewControllerDescriptors()** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:495`): All controllers are registered in `NewControllerDescriptors()`, which collects every `ControllerDescriptor` into a map keyed by controller name. Each file (core.go, apps.go, batch.go, networking.go, etc.) contributes descriptors via `newXxxControllerDescriptor()` factory functions.\\n\\n4. **Manager Context — ControllerContext** (`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/controllercontext.go` and `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:594`): `CreateControllerContext` builds a `ControllerContext` struct containing shared informers (`InformerFactory`), a client builder, REST mapper, and other resources — this is the equivalent of the controller-runtime `Manager`.\\n\\n5. **Wiring into the reconcile loop — Run() → StartControllers() → StartController()** (`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`): The top-level `Run()` function calls `NewControllerDescriptors()` to get all registered controllers, creates the `ControllerContext`, then calls `StartControllers()`. `StartControllers()` iterates over the descriptor map and calls `StartController()` for each, which invokes the `InitFunc`. The `InitFunc` instantiates the controller and spawns its run goroutine.\\n\\n6. **Controller Reconcile Loop** (e.g., `pkg/controller/endpoint/endpoints_controller.go`, `pkg/controller/storageversionmigrator/storageversionmigrator.go`): Each controller implements a `Run(ctx, workers)` method that starts multiple goroutines calling `worker()`, which dequeues items from a rate-limited workqueue and calls the internal `syncXxx()` method — the actual reconcile function.\\n\\n7. **Generic Policy Controller Pattern** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/internal/generic/controller.go`): The admission policy subsystem defines its own generic `Controller[T]` interface and `controller[T]` implementation with a `reconciler func(namespace, name string, newObj T) error` callback — a more direct analogue to controller-runtime's Reconciler interface. `NewController()` is the equivalent of `SetupWithManager`, and `Run()` drives the reconcile loop.\"\n}\nEOF","description":"Write answer.json"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1488,"cache_read_input_tokens":63495,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1488,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"87266e37-4c1e-47fc-848b-9d29224d1f72","uuid":"cc08f80e-3fe4-4eea-9ddd-1ca0701f5c72"}

Reconciler Interface\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go`**\n- `controller.Interface` — base interface requiring `Name() string` (analogous to `reconcile.Reconciler`)\n- Optional: `Debuggable`, `HealthCheckable` interfaces\n\n### 2. Registration\n**`cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:495`** — `NewControllerDescriptors()` collects all controller descriptors into a map; each controller file (core.go, apps.go, batch.go, etc.) contributes its descriptors.\n\n### 4.
